name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Superior King Room
info:Stayed in December 2023
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted December 10, 2023
msg:The hotel service is very good. After booking, Xiao Luo, the front desk clerk, called in advance to ask about our room preferences. Knowing that my wife and I were taking advantage of the weekend to bring our children to celebrate our anniversary, we found a surprise when we arrived at the hotel - not only did they arrange a room with a good view for us, but they also decorated our room with a small tent, children's toiletries, etc., and also folded two big and beautiful swans. My wife and children love it! Thank you Xiao Luo for the arrangement, and praise the room attendant for his ingenuity!
The hotel is very close to the highway exit, but the hotel entrance is not particularly obvious. I drove past it and then turned back. The hotel itself is very beautiful, with European-style buildings. It can be seen that there are some buildings with a very unified style around it, including outlets, but after a walk, it feels that the construction around the hotel has been abandoned by Greenland, and there is no popularity. The hotel is probably struggling.
Back to the point, the hotel is very stylish, free parking, and there are many parking spaces. The room is large, spacious and bright, the air conditioning effect is very good, very warm, the bedding is particularly comfortable, and there is a large sofa. The hotel also has a gym and a heated swimming pool.
We had breakfast and buffet dinner at the hotel. The breakfast was rich in variety and tasted very good. The tofu pudding was delicious and the beef noodle soup was very solid. The buffet dinner had a small hot pot, which turned out to be a chicken soup hot pot. The soup was delicious and the side dishes were rich. There were also seafood (crabs and shrimps were delicious), various sashimi (salmon, tuna, etc., a sashimi platter is totally fine), various dim sum desserts (many varieties, beautiful shapes, durian mille-feuille and ice cream), various hot dishes (grilled big elbows, freshly fried steaks were particularly fragrant, and there was even Peking duck). In short, it was very worthwhile! I will come again in the future.
----------------------------------------
